being a full-time nostalgia strip about the wonderful world of comics and the people who love them, Dick is apparently going to appear at a cosplay convention, presumably cosplaying as Dick Tracy. Remember when this strip was about gimp-masked serial killers being <a href=\"https://joshreads.com/2011/03/monday-post/#eaten\" target=\"_blank\">eaten alive by rats</a>?
